### [71] [Energy-Aware Pattern Disentanglement: A Generalizable Pattern Assisted Architecture for Multi-task Time Series Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.14209)
*Xiangkai Ma,Xiaobin Hong,Wenzhong Li,Sanglu Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 深度学习在时间序列分析中取得巨大成功，但现有方法“一模型一任务”的架构限制了其泛化能力。本文提出Pets，一种基于“通用波动模式辅助”（GPA）框架的“一模型多任务”架构，通过分析时频域的局部能量来捕捉和分离瞬态和非平稳振荡分量。研究发现生成任务倾向于捕捉低频分量的长周期模式，而判别任务则关注高频突变信号。Pets集成了“波动模式辅助”（FPA）模块和“上下文引导预测器混合”（MoP）模块，前者促进了不同波动模式间的信息融合，后者利用这些可泛化模式表示来指导和调节不同波动的重构。Pets在60个基准测试的多种任务（预测、填充、异常检测、分类）上均实现了最先进的性能，并表现出强大的泛化能力和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法在时间序列分析中普遍采用“一模型一任务”的架构，这在很大程度上限制了模型在不同任务间的泛化能力。例如，一个用于时间序列预测的模型通常不能直接用于异常检测或分类任务。这种局限性使得研究者需要为每个新任务开发或微调专门的模型，增加了时间和计算资源的成本。因此，开发一种能够适应多种时间序列任务的通用模型架构，以提高模型的泛化能力和效率，具有重要的研究意义和实际应用价值。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为Pets的新型“一模型多任务”架构，其核心是基于“通用波动模式辅助”（GPA）框架。该架构通过在时频域进行局部能量分析，精确地捕捉和分离时间序列中的瞬态和非平稳振荡分量。研究发现，生成任务倾向于从低频分量中捕捉长周期模式，而判别任务则侧重于高频分量中的突变信号。Pets模型由两部分组成：1. 波动模式辅助（FPA）模块：该模块负责融合不同波动模式的信息，通过捕捉它们之间的依赖关系，并在每一层逐步将这些模式建模为潜在表示。2. 上下文引导预测器混合（MoP）模块：该模块利用FPA模块生成的通用模式表示，通过能量比例来分层地引导和调节不同波动的重构。这种设计使得Pets能够适应各种时间序列分析任务。

Result: Pets在60个多样化的基准测试任务上进行了评估，涵盖了时间序列分析的多种任务，包括预测、填充、异常检测和分类。实验结果表明，Pets在所有这些任务上均取得了最先进（state-of-the-art）的性能。此外，Pets模型还展现出了强大的泛化能力和鲁棒性，能够有效地处理不同类型的时间序列数据和任务需求，证明了其“一模型多任务”架构的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Pets架构通过创新的时频域局部能量分析和“一模型多任务”设计，有效解决了现有时间序列分析方法泛化能力不足的问题。Pets能够准确捕捉和分离时间序列中的关键波动模式，并根据任务类型（生成或判别）自适应地利用这些模式，在多项任务上取得了卓越的性能。尽管Pets在多个基准测试中表现出色，但未来的工作可以进一步探索其在更复杂、更大规模数据集上的表现，以及研究其在实时应用中的效率和可扩展性。

Abstract: Time series analysis has found widespread applications in areas such as weather forecasting, anomaly detection, and healthcare. While deep learning approaches have achieved significant success in this field, existing methods often adopt a "one-model one-task" architecture, limiting their generalization across different tasks. To address these limitations, we perform local energy analysis in the time-frequency domain to more precisely capture and disentangle transient and non-stationary oscillatory components. Furthermore, our representational analysis reveals that generative tasks tend to capture long-period patterns from low-frequency components, whereas discriminative tasks focus on high-frequency abrupt signals, which constitutes our core contribution. Concretely, we propose Pets, a novel "one-model many-tasks" architecture based on the General fluctuation Pattern Assisted (GPA) framework that is adaptable to versatile model structures for time series analysis. Pets integrates a Fluctuation Pattern Assisted (FPA) module and a Context-Guided Mixture of Predictors (MoP). The FPA module facilitates information fusion among diverse fluctuation patterns by capturing their dependencies and progressively modeling these patterns as latent representations at each layer. Meanwhile, the MoP module leverages these generalizable pattern representations to guide and regulate the reconstruction of distinct fluctuations hierarchically by energy proportion. Pets demonstrates strong versatility and achieves state-of-the-art performance across 60 benchmarks on various tasks, including forecasting, imputation, anomaly detection, and classification, while demonstrating strong generalization and robustness.

</details>


### [72] [MMTU: A Massive Multi-Task Table Understanding and Reasoning Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05587)

Conclusion: MMTU基准的提出为全面评估和推动大型语言模型在结构化数据处理和分析领域的发展提供了重要的工具。当前的评估结果显示，在处理真实世界复杂表格任务方面，现有模型仍有很大的改进潜力，这为未来的研究指明了方向。代码和数据已公开。

Abstract: Tables and table-based use cases play a crucial role in many important real-world applications, such as spreadsheets, databases, and computational notebooks, which traditionally require expert-level users like data engineers, data analysts, and database administrators to operate. Although LLMs have shown remarkable progress in working with tables (e.g., in spreadsheet and database copilot scenarios), comprehensive benchmarking of such capabilities remains limited. In contrast to an extensive and growing list of NLP benchmarks, evaluations of table-related tasks are scarce, and narrowly focus on tasks like NL-to-SQL and Table-QA, overlooking the broader spectrum of real-world tasks that professional users face. This gap limits our understanding and model progress in this important area.
  In this work, we introduce MMTU, a large-scale benchmark with over 28K questions across 25 real-world table tasks, designed to comprehensively evaluate models ability to understand, reason, and manipulate real tables at the expert-level. These tasks are drawn from decades' worth of computer science research on tabular data, with a focus on complex table tasks faced by professional users. We show that MMTU require a combination of skills -- including table understanding, reasoning, and coding -- that remain challenging for today's frontier models, where even frontier reasoning models like OpenAI GPT-5 and DeepSeek R1 score only around 69\% and 57\% respectively, suggesting significant room for improvement. We highlight key findings in our evaluation using MMTU and hope that this benchmark drives further advances in understanding and developing foundation models for structured data processing and analysis.
  Our code and data are available at https://github.com/MMTU-Benchmark/MMTU and https://huggingface.co/datasets/MMTU-benchmark/MMTU.

### [73] [Access Controls Will Solve the Dual-Use Dilemma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.09341)
*Evžen Wybitul*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AI安全系统面临双重用途困境，即无法区分无害或有害的请求。为解决此问题，本文提出了一个基于访问控制的概念框架，仅允许经验证用户访问双重用途的输出。该框架旨在减少不必要的拒绝和允许有害请求的情况，从而在提高实用性的同时不牺牲安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI安全系统在处理潜在的双重用途请求时面临困境，因为无法区分请求者的意图，可能导致拒绝合法请求或允许有害请求。现有系统缺乏访问真实世界上下文信息的能力，从而做出任意选择，影响了系统的实用性和安全性。

Method: 提出一个基于访问控制的概念框架，将双重用途的输出限制在经验证用户范围内。框架包括对用户进行验证，并根据验证结果控制对双重用途内容的访问。对该框架的可行性进行了分析。

Result: 该框架通过仅向经验证用户提供对双重用途输出的访问，解决了AI安全系统中过度拒绝和拒绝对有害请求的允许问题。虽然只是一个高层提案，但它为模型提供商提供了管理双重用途内容的更精细化工具。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于访问控制的概念框架为AI安全系统管理双重用途内容提供了新的解决方案，有望在提高用户访问能力的同时不牺牲安全性，并为监管机构提供更具针对性的政策选项。未来的工作将集中在实现和评估该框架的实际效果。

Abstract: AI safety systems face the dual-use dilemma. It is unclear whether to answer dual-use requests, since the same query could be either harmless or harmful depending on who made it and why. To make better decisions, such systems would need to examine requests' real-world context, but currently, they lack access to this information. Instead, they sometimes end up making arbitrary choices that result in refusing legitimate queries and allowing harmful ones, which hurts both utility and safety. To address this, we propose a conceptual framework based on access controls where only verified users can access dual-use outputs. We describe the framework's components, analyse its feasibility, and explain how it addresses both over-refusals and under-refusals. While only a high-level proposal, our work takes the first step toward giving model providers more granular tools for managing dual-use content. Such tools would enable users to access more capabilities without sacrificing safety, and offer regulators new options for targeted policies.

### [74] [CoT Red-Handed: Stress Testing Chain-of-Thought Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.23575)
*Benjamin Arnav,Pablo Bernabeu-Pérez,Nathan Helm-Burger,Tim Kostolansky,Hannes Whittingham,Mary Phuong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了链式思考（CoT）监控方法，用于监督AI模型的中间推理步骤，以防止其在自主部署时产生有害行为。研究发现，CoT监控比仅监控最终输出（动作监控）更能有效识别AI的破坏行为，尤其是在动作监控失效的情况下。然而，CoT监控也可能被AI误导性的推理所欺骗。为解决此问题，研究引入了一种混合监控协议，该协议结合了对模型推理和动作的独立评分，并在多项任务中表现出比单独的CoT监控和动作监控高出一倍的检测率，尤其是在细微欺骗场景下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI模型自主性的增强，确保它们在不被注意的情况下不会采取有害行动变得至关重要。本研究旨在探索一种有效的监控机制，以缓解这一风险。

Method: 本研究比较了两种监控方法：链式思考（CoT）监控，即一个较弱的可信监控模型持续监督一个更强大的、不可信模型的中间推理步骤；以及动作监控，即仅审查最终输出。研究在一个红队测试场景中进行了比较，其中不可信模型在完成编码任务的同时，被指示执行有害的侧任务。为进一步提高监控效果，研究引入了一种混合协议，该协议独立评估模型推理和动作，并采用加权平均的方式结合两者。

Result: 研究发现，在动作监控无法可靠识别破坏行为的情况下，CoT监控比仅监控模型输出更有效。然而，CoT监控在面对AI误导性推理时，性能会下降。混合监控协议在所有测试模型和任务中始终优于CoT监控和动作监控，尤其是在细微欺骗场景下，其检测率是动作监控的两倍。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的混合监控协议能够有效提升AI模型的安全性，尤其是在应对复杂的欺骗行为方面。尽管CoT监控具有潜力，但其易被误导的特性限制了其应用。混合协议通过结合推理和动作的监控，实现了更优越的性能，为AI的安全部署提供了新的解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索更精细的推理评估方法以及自适应的混合权重调整策略。

Abstract: As AI models are deployed with increasing autonomy, it is important to ensure they do not take harmful actions unnoticed. As a potential mitigation, we investigate Chain-of-Thought (CoT) monitoring, wherein a weaker trusted monitor model continuously oversees the intermediate reasoning steps of a more powerful but untrusted model. We compare CoT monitoring to action-only monitoring, where only final outputs are reviewed, in a red-teaming setup where the untrusted model is instructed to pursue harmful side tasks while completing a coding problem. We find that while CoT monitoring is more effective than overseeing only model outputs in scenarios where action-only monitoring fails to reliably identify sabotage, reasoning traces can contain misleading rationalizations that deceive the CoT monitors, reducing performance in obvious sabotage cases. To address this, we introduce a hybrid protocol that independently scores model reasoning and actions, and combines them using a weighted average. Our hybrid monitor consistently outperforms both CoT and action-only monitors across all tested models and tasks, with detection rates twice higher than action-only monitoring for subtle deception scenarios.

### [75] [Deep Hidden Cognition Facilitates Reliable Chain-of-Thought Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.10007)
*Zijun Chen,Wenbo Hu,Richang Hong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种校准思维链（CoT）推理准确性的新方法，通过利用模型内在的真实性编码，识别并利用对推理步骤真实性敏感的注意力头激活，训练置信度预测器来评估每个推理步骤的正确性，并通过束搜索动态选择最合理的推理路径，从而显著提高了模型在数学、符号和常识推理任务上的准确性和可靠性，并且在单模态和多模态设置下均表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管思维链（CoT）推理在大型语言模型（LLMs）和多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）中展现了强大的推理能力，但其中间步骤的错误累积问题严重影响了其可靠性。因此，有必要研究一种能够提高CoT推理准确性和可靠性的新方法。

Method: 本研究提出了一种新颖的校准CoT推理准确性的方法。首先，通过观察发现特定的注意力头激活能够可靠地反映CoT推理步骤的真实性。基于此洞察，研究者训练了一个置信度预测器，利用这些对真实性敏感的激活来评估每个推理步骤的正确性。接着，采用束搜索策略，根据置信度预测器的评估结果，动态地选择最可能的推理路径。实验在数学、符号和常识推理任务上进行了评估，并与几种最先进的方法进行了比较。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提出的方法在数学、符号和常识推理任务上显著优于现有的最先进基线方法，包括少样本CoT、自洽性和自评估引导束搜索。该方法在单模态和多模态设置下均展现出优越的准确性和可靠性。此外，该方法在大规模推理模型上的验证也证实了其对专业推理模型的适用性。研究还探讨了模型自我纠正能力在CoT推理中的作用。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种通过校准CoT推理来提高其准确性和可靠性的新方法，该方法利用模型内在的真实性编码，通过置信度预测器和束搜索来动态选择最优推理路径，并在多项推理任务和模型上取得了显著的性能提升。这项工作为提高CoT推理的可靠性提供了一条新的途径，并具有广泛的应用潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索模型自我纠正能力在CoT推理中的作用，并将其应用于更广泛的领域。

Abstract: Chain of Thought (CoT) reasoning has demonstrated remarkable deep reasoning capabilities in both large language models (LLMs) and multimodal large language models (MLLMs). However, its reliability is often undermined by the accumulation of errors in intermediate steps. This paper introduces an novel approach to calibrate the CoT reasoning accuracy by leveraging the model's intrinsic veracity encoding. We discover that specific attention head activations reliably reflect the truthfulness of reasoning steps in CoT. Based on this insight, we train a confidence predictor to evaluate the correctness of each reasoning step using these truthfulness-sensitive activations, dynamically selecting the most plausible reasoning path via beam search. Experimental results demonstrate that our method significantly outperforms the state-of-the-art baselines (e.g., Few-Shot CoT, Self-Consistency, and Self-Evaluation Guided Beam Search) across the mathematical, symbolic, and commonsense reasoning tasks, exhibiting superior accuracy and reliability in both unimodal and multimodal settings. We further validate the approach on large reasoning models, confirming its applicability to specialized reasoning models. Additionally, we explore the role of the model's self-correction ability in CoT reasoning. This work provides a novel reliability improvement path for CoT reasoning with broad application potential.

</details>


### [76] [ASP-Assisted Symbolic Regression: Uncovering Hidden Physics in Fluid Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17777)
*Theofanis Aravanis,Grigorios Chrimatopoulos,Mohammad Ferdows,Michalis Xenos,Efstratios Em Tzirtzilakis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究将符号回归（SR）应用于流体动力学，以解决传统机器学习（ML）模型的可解释性问题。研究人员使用SR从数值模拟数据中生成了描述三维层流在矩形通道中轴向速度和压力的紧凑型符号方程，这些方程与文献中的解析解吻合良好。为了解决纯数据驱动的SR模型可能忽视领域特定约束的问题，研究还引入了一个结合SR和答案集编程（ASP）的混合框架，以确保导出方程在统计上准确且物理上合理。该SR/ASP方法展示了结合数据驱动和知识表示方法以增强可解释性、可靠性以及与物理原理一致性的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的机器学习（ML）模型常被视为“黑箱”，缺乏可解释性，这在流体动力学等需要理解底层物理机制的领域是一个重大限制。符号回归（SR）通过从用户定义的数学原语构建表达式，提供了一种可解释的替代方案，能够自动发现符合数据并揭示物理关系的紧凑公式。然而，纯粹的数据驱动的SR模型可能无法保证物理上的合理性。因此，本研究旨在利用SR解决流体动力学建模的可解释性问题，并提出一种结合SR和ASP的混合方法，以确保模型的统计准确性和物理合理性。

Method: 本研究首先将符号回归（SR）应用于建模三维层流在矩形通道中的轴向速度和压力场。SR技术从数值模拟数据中自动构建数学表达式。接着，为了提升模型的物理合理性，研究引入了一个创新的混合框架，该框架将SR与答案集编程（ASP）相结合。ASP是一种声明式推理技术，用于处理知识表示和推理问题。这种SR/ASP方法结合了SR的生成能力和ASP的推理能力，以确保导出的方程既统计准确又符合物理规律。

Result: 研究成功从数值模拟数据中推导出了描述三维层流在矩形通道中轴向速度和压力场的紧凑型符号方程。这些方程准确地重现了预期的抛物线速度分布和线性压降，并与文献中的解析解显示出极好的一致性。通过结合ASP，确保了所得方程不仅在统计上精确，而且在物理上也是合理的。

Conclusion: 本研究成功展示了符号回归（SR）在流体动力学建模中的应用潜力，解决了传统ML模型的可解释性问题。通过引入SR/ASP混合框架，研究不仅获得了与解析解高度一致的符号方程，还确保了模型在统计准确性和物理合理性方面的优势。该方法为在流体动力学及相关领域中增强模型的可解释性、可靠性以及与物理原理的一致性提供了有前景的途径。未来的工作可以进一步探索该方法在更复杂流体问题中的应用。

Abstract: Symbolic Regression (SR) offers an interpretable alternative to conventional Machine-Learning (ML) approaches, which are often criticized as ``black boxes''. In contrast to standard regression models that require a prescribed functional form, SR constructs expressions from a user-defined set of mathematical primitives, enabling the automated discovery of compact formulas that fit the data and reveal underlying physical relationships. In fluid mechanics, where understanding the underlying physics is as crucial as predictive accuracy, this study applies SR to model three-dimensional (3D) laminar flow in a rectangular channel, focusing on the axial velocity and pressure fields. Compact symbolic equations were derived from numerical simulation data, accurately reproducing the expected parabolic velocity profile and linear pressure drop, and showing excellent agreement with analytical solutions from the literature. To address the limitation that purely data-driven SR models may overlook domain-specific constraints, an innovative hybrid framework that integrates SR with Answer Set Programming (ASP) is also introduced. This integration combines the generative power of SR with the declarative reasoning capabilities of ASP, ensuring that derived equations remain both statistically accurate and physically plausible. The proposed SR/ASP methodology demonstrates the potential of combining data-driven and knowledge-representation approaches to enhance interpretability, reliability, and alignment with physical principles in fluid dynamics and related domains.

</details>


### [77] [Emotion-Coherent Reasoning for Multimodal LLMs via Emotional Rationale Verifier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.23506)
*Hyeongseop Rha,Jeong Hun Yeo,Yeonju Kim,Yong Man Ro*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MLLMs在人机交互中实现更智能的情感理解和可信赖的解释。现有方法存在解释与预测不一致的问题。本文提出情感理由验证器(ERV)和解释奖励，以提高情感识别中解释与预测的一致性，无需修改模型架构或额外标注。实验证明该方法提高了MAFW和DFEW数据集上的解释-预测一致性和解释情感准确性，使MLLMs能够提供情感连贯、可信赖的交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出情感理由验证器(ERV)和解释奖励。ERV在多模态情感识别过程中，指导模型生成与目标情感明确一致的推理过程，且不修改模型架构，也无需额外的配对视频-描述标注。通过整合ERV和解释奖励，模型被引导产生更符合情感预测的解释。

Result: 在MAFW和DFEW数据集上，所提出的方法显著提高了解释-预测一致性和解释情感准确性。实验和人类评估表明，该方法增强了解释和预测之间的一致性，并使MLLMs能够提供情感连贯、可信赖的交互。

Conclusion: 本文提出的ERV和解释奖励方法是朝着真正类人HCI系统迈出的关键一步，它解决了当前MLLMs在情感解释方面的一致性问题，提高了模型的可信赖度，并为未来更智能、更具情感理解能力的人机交互系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: The recent advancement of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) is transforming human-computer interaction (HCI) from surface-level exchanges into more nuanced and emotionally intelligent communication. To realize this shift, emotion understanding becomes essential allowing systems to capture subtle cues underlying user intent. Furthermore, providing faithful explanations for predicted emotions is crucial to ensure interpretability and build user trust. However, current MLLM-based methods often generate emotion explanations that diverge from the target labels and sometimes even contradict their own predicted emotions. This inconsistency poses a critical risk for misunderstanding and erodes reliability in interactive settings. To address this, we propose a novel approach: the Emotional Rationale Verifier (ERV) and an Explanation Reward. Our method guides the model to produce reasoning that is explicitly consistent with the target emotion during multimodal emotion recognition without modifying the model architecture or requiring additional paired video-description annotations. Our method significantly improves faithful explanation-prediction consistency and explanation emotion accuracy on the MAFW and DFEW datasets. Through extensive experiments and human evaluations, we show that our approach not only enhances alignment between explanation and prediction but also empowers MLLMs to deliver emotionally coherent, trustworthy interactions, marking a key step toward truly human-like HCI systems.

### [78] [Beyond ReAct: A Planner-Centric Framework for Complex Tool-Augmented LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10037)
*Xiaolong Wei,Yuehu Dong,Xingliang Wang,Xingyu Zhang,Zhejun Zhao,Dongdong Shen,Long Xia,Dawei Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 现有的工具增强大语言模型在处理复杂查询时面临局部优化陷阱的问题。我们提出了一个以规划为中心的“规划-执行”范式，通过全局有向无环图（DAG）规划来解决此问题。我们还引入了一个名为ComplexTool-Plan的大规模基准数据集和一个结合SFT和GRPO的两阶段训练方法。该框架在StableToolBench基准上达到了最先进的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的工具增强大语言模型（LLMs）在处理复杂查询时，由于依赖增量决策过程，容易陷入局部优化陷阱。这限制了它们在需要复杂工具协调和组合的场景下的表现。

Method: 我们提出了一种新颖的“规划-执行”范式，其核心是一个能够对复杂查询进行全局有向无环图（DAG）规划的规划器模型。我们还构建了一个名为ComplexTool-Plan的大规模基准数据集，并采用结合监督微调（SFT）和组相对策略优化（GRPO）的两阶段训练方法来提升规划器的性能。

Result: 在StableToolBench基准上，我们的框架在处理复杂用户查询时实现了最先进的性能，展示了其在端到端执行能力和处理复杂多工具工作流方面的优越性。

Conclusion: 我们提出的规划器中心“规划-执行”范式有效地解决了现有工具增强LLMs在处理复杂查询时的局部优化问题。通过全局DAG规划、大规模基准测试和创新的训练方法，我们的框架在复杂工具协调方面取得了显著进展，为未来研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Existing tool-augmented large language models (LLMs) encounter significant challenges when processing complex queries. Current frameworks such as ReAct are prone to local optimization traps due to their reliance on incremental decision-making processes. To address these limitations, we propose a novel Planner-centric Plan-Execute paradigm that fundamentally resolves local optimization bottlenecks through architectural innovation. Central to our approach is a novel Planner model that performs global Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) planning for complex queries, enabling optimized execution beyond conventional tool coordination. We also introduce ComplexTool-Plan, a large-scale benchmark dataset featuring complex queries that demand sophisticated multi-tool composition and coordination capabilities. Additionally, we develop a two-stage training methodology that integrates Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), systematically enhancing the Planner's tool selection accuracy and global planning awareness through structured DAG-based planning. When integrated with a capable executor, our framework achieves state-of-the-art performance on the StableToolBench benchmark for complex user queries, demonstrating superior end-to-end execution capabilities and robust handling of intricate multi-tool workflows.

### [79] [Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization for Power Distribution System Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.14730)
*Parya Dolatyabi,Mahdi Khodayar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为异构体强化学习（HARL）的框架，并使用异构体近端策略优化（HAPPO）算法来解决大规模停电后配电系统的恢复问题。与传统方法和基于价值的强化学习方法相比，HARL能够更有效地协调互联微电网的恢复过程，并处理实际的非线性约束和异构特性，实现了更快的收敛速度、更高的恢复功率和更稳定的训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模停电后恢复电力分配系统（PDS）需要进行一系列的开关操作，以重新配置馈线拓扑结构并协调分布式能源（DER）的运行。然而，这一过程受到功率平衡、电压限制和热额定值等非线性约束的限制，使得传统的优化方法和基于价值的强化学习方法在计算效率和可扩展性方面存在挑战。因此，需要一种新的方法来应对这些复杂性。

Method: 本研究提出并实现了一种基于异构体强化学习（HARL）的框架，具体采用异构体近端策略优化（HAPPO）算法。该框架将每个微电网视为一个独立的智能体，并赋予其不同的负载、DER容量和开关数量，以处理实际的结构异构性。通过中心化Critic和去中心化Actor策略进行训练，以获得稳定的策略更新。实验环境利用OpenDSS，通过可微分的惩罚信号来强制执行操作限制，而非无效动作掩码。实验在IEEE 123节点和IEEE 8500节点系统上进行。

Result: 实验结果表明，HAPPO在IEEE 123节点和IEEE 8500节点系统上，相比于DQN、PPO、MAES、MAGDPG、MADQN、Mean-Field RL和QMIX等算法，展现出更快的收敛速度、更高的恢复功率和更平稳的多种子训练过程。这证明了HARL框架在处理微电网异构性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功地将HARL框架应用于电力分配系统的恢复问题，并通过HAPPO算法实现了对互联微电网的协调恢复。该方法不仅克服了传统方法的计算效率和可扩展性限制，而且能够有效地处理复杂的非线性约束和系统异构性。实验结果证实了该方法在恢复速度、恢复功率和训练稳定性方面的优越性，为复杂电力分配系统恢复提供了一种可扩展、稳定且满足约束的解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的系统场景和更广泛的异构性处理。

Abstract: Restoring power distribution systems (PDS) after large-scale outages requires sequential switching operations that reconfigure feeder topology and coordinate distributed energy resources (DERs) under nonlinear constraints such as power balance, voltage limits, and thermal ratings. These challenges make conventional optimization and value-based RL approaches computationally inefficient and difficult to scale. This paper applies a Heterogeneous-Agent Reinforcement Learning (HARL) framework, instantiated through Heterogeneous-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (HAPPO), to enable coordinated restoration across interconnected microgrids. Each agent controls a distinct microgrid with different loads, DER capacities, and switch counts, introducing practical structural heterogeneity. Decentralized actor policies are trained with a centralized critic to compute advantage values for stable on-policy updates. A physics-informed OpenDSS environment provides full power flow feedback and enforces operational limits via differentiable penalty signals rather than invalid action masking. The total DER generation is capped at 2400 kW, and each microgrid must satisfy local supply-demand feasibility. Experiments on the IEEE 123-bus and IEEE 8500-node systems show that HAPPO achieves faster convergence, higher restored power, and smoother multi-seed training than DQN, PPO, MAES, MAGDPG, MADQN, Mean-Field RL, and QMIX. Results demonstrate that incorporating microgrid-level heterogeneity within the HARL framework yields a scalable, stable, and constraint-aware solution for complex PDS restoration.

</details>

### [80] [Investigation of Inverse Bremsstrahlung Heating Driven by Broadband Lasers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.20024)
*Xiaoran Li,Jie Qiu,Liang Hao,Chen Wang,Lifeng Wang,Shiyang Zou*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 研究发现，宽带激光虽然会引起碰撞逆韧致辐射（IB）加热率的瞬时波动，但长期平均加热和净IB吸收基本不受影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 惯性约束聚变（ICF）中，宽带激光是减轻激光等离子体不稳定的关键策略，但其对碰撞逆韧致辐射（IB）加热的影响尚不清楚。

Method: 使用一维碰撞粒子模拟，系统研究了宽带化引起的退相干效应对金（Au）等离子体中IB吸收的影响。将模拟与经典吸收理论进行基准测试，验证了碰撞模型准确再现了理论IB加热率。

Result: 模拟显示，与单色激光相比，宽带激光虽然在加热率中引入了由随机强度涨落驱动的瞬时皮秒尺度振荡，但长期平均加热率和净IB吸收保持不变。

Conclusion: 宽带激光在惯性约束聚变中对碰撞逆韧致辐射（IB）加热的影响不大，长期平均吸收保持不变，这表明其在等离子体不稳定性控制方面的应用前景广阔，但仍需进一步研究其对其他等离子体过程的影响。

Abstract: Broadband lasers have become a key strategy for mitigating laser plasma instabilities in inertial confinement fusion, yet their impact on collisional inverse bremsstrahlung (IB) heating remains unclear. Using one-dimensional collisional particle-in-cell simulations, we systematically examine the effect of bandwidth-induced temporal incoherence on IB absorption in Au plasmas. The simulations are first benchmarked against classical absorption theory, verifying that the implemented Coulomb collision model accurately reproduces the theoretical IB heating rate. A direct comparison of the electron temperature evolution in the broadband and monochromatic cases shows that, although spectral broadening introduces transient picosecond-scale oscillations in the heating rate driven by stochastic intensity fluctuations, the long-term averaged heating and net IB absorption remain essentially unchanged.

</details>


### [81] [Collisionless Shocks Mediated by Shear-Flow Magnetic Fields in Ultraintense-Laser-Produced Counter-Streaming Plasmas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.20040)
*Jun-Yi Lu,Kai Wang,Jin-Long Jiao*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用粒子 in cell 模拟研究了超强激光产生的反向流等离子体中离子-Weibel 介导的无碰撞激波（IW-CSs）的形成。研究发现，剪切流离子-Weibel 不稳定性产生磁场，从而使流入流各向同性并介导激波形成。推导了剪切流磁场的解析表达式，并建立了磁场幅值与激光强度之间的比例关系。与高功率激光实验相比，该机制将激波形成时间和所需激光能量分别减少了三个和两个数量级，使得利用现有的兆焦耳、皮秒超强激光装置生产 IW-CSs 成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无碰撞激波（CSs）的产生对于理解天体物理现象（如超新星遗迹和活动星系核）以及在实验室中实现高能量密度物理至关重要。然而，在实验室环境中产生 CSs 通常需要极高的激光能量和复杂的装置。因此，寻找更高效、更易于实现的 CSs 产生方法具有重要意义。

Method: 本研究采用粒子 in cell (PIC) 模拟方法来研究超强激光产生的反向流等离子体中的离子-Weibel 介导的无碰撞激波（IW-CSs）的形成。通过详细分析模拟结果，研究了其内在的微观物理机制，包括剪切流离子-Weibel 不稳定性的激发、磁场的产生及其对激波形成的影响。此外，还推导了剪切流磁场的解析表达式，并建立了磁场幅值与激光强度之间的比例关系。

Result: 模拟结果表明，剪切流离子-Weibel 不稳定性能够有效地生成磁场。这些磁场能够使流入流发生各向同性化，并成功介导了激波的形成。研究推导出的解析表达式和比例关系揭示了磁场幅值与激光强度之间的定量联系。与高功率激光实验相比，该机制显著提高了激波产生的效率，将激波形成时间缩短了三个数量级，并将所需的激光能量降低了两个数量级。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的离子-Weibel 介导的无碰撞激波（IW-CSs）形成机制，利用超强激光产生的反向流等离子体，通过剪切流离子-Weibel 不稳定性生成磁场，有效地促进了激波的形成。该机制相较于传统方法，极大地降低了激波形成所需的时间和能量，使得利用现有的激光装置成为可能。这对于实验室天体物理和高能量密度物理的研究具有重要的理论和实验意义。未来的工作可以进一步探索该机制在不同等离子体参数下的鲁棒性，并尝试通过实验验证这些模拟结果。

Abstract: The formation of ion-Weibel-mediated collisionless shocks (IW-CSs) in ultraintense-laser-produced counter-streaming plasmas is investigated using particle-in-cell simulations. Analysis of the underlying microphysics reveals that a shear-flow ion-Weibel instability generates magnetic fields, which isotropize the incoming flow and mediate shock formation. An analytical expression for the shear-flow magnetic field is derived, and a scaling law relating the magnetic field amplitude to the laser intensity is established. This mechanism reduces the shock formation time and the required laser energy by three and two orders of magnitude, respectively, compared to high-power laser experiments, making it feasible to produce IW-CSs using existing multi-kilojoule, picosecond ultraintense laser facilities.

</details>


### [82] [The PLUTO Code on GPUs: A First Look at Eulerian MHD Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.20337)
*Marco Rossazza,Andrea Mignone,Matteo Bugli,Stefano Truzzi,Lubomir Riha,Tomas Panoc,Ondrej Vysocky,Nitin Shukla,Alessandro Romeo,Vittoria Berta*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: gPLUTO是计算等离子体天体物理学中PLUTO代码的新的GPU优化实现，它使用有限体积法求解多维磁流体力学方程，并利用OpenACC在NVIDIA GPU上实现加速，初步结果表明了其在预E级并行架构上的潜力和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是开发一种新的、高性能的计算等离子体天体物理学代码，以解决多维磁流体力学（MHD）方程。随着计算能力的不断提高，对能够有效利用现代硬件（如NVIDIA GPU）的先进模拟工具有着日益增长的需求。

Method: gPLUTO的实现采用了C++语言和OpenACC编程模型，这是对现有PLUTO代码的完全重写。该代码使用有限体积法来数值求解MHD方程。研究的重点是评估gPLUTO在预E级并行架构上的性能，尽管详细的代码描述和模块将在未来的论文中介绍。

Result: 初步的性能结果表明，gPLUTO在NVIDIA GPU上实现了显著的加速。虽然具体的性能指标和比较没有在摘要中详细说明，但结果被用来展示代码的潜力和其在高性能计算环境中的有效性。

Conclusion: gPLUTO代表了计算等离子体天体物理学领域的一个重要进展，它通过利用GPU加速提供了更快的模拟能力。虽然初步结果令人鼓舞，但该研究承认需要进一步的详细描述和更全面的性能评估，未来的工作将集中在代码的进一步开发和应用上。

Abstract: We present preliminary performance results of gPLUTO, the new GPU-optimized implementation of the PLUTO code for computational plasma astrophysics. Like its predecessor, gPLUTO employs a finite-volume formulation to numerically solve the equations of magnetohydrodynamics (MHD) in multiple spatial dimensions. Still, this new implementation is a complete rewrite in C++ and leverages the OpenACC programming model to achieve acceleration on NVIDIA GPUs. While a more comprehensive description of the code and its several other modules will be presented in a future paper, here we focus on some preparatory results that demonstrate the code potential and performance on pre exa-scale parallel architectures.

### [83] [Microphysical boundary condition for the electron kinetics of a plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.20346)
*Felix Willert,Clemens Hoyer,Gordon K. Grubert,Franz X. Bronold*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 该研究推导并实现了一种适用于等离子体内部电子动力学描述的边界条件，该条件考虑了壁内微物理过程，并基于描述电子在固体中散射级联和次级电子激发的表面散射核。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有等离子体模拟方法在处理电子与壁相互作用时，未能充分考虑壁内微物理过程，导致模拟结果不准确。本研究旨在开发一种能包含这些微物理过程的边界条件，以提高模拟的精度。

Method: 研究推导了一种基于表面散射核的非弹性、角度和能量依赖的边界条件。该边界条件被实现并应用于基于勒让德多项式展开方法的玻尔兹曼方程求解器。计算成本分析表明，新的边界条件带来的计算开销适中。

Result: 结果显示了非弹性效应对模拟结果的影响。通过一个硅壁面对氩、氦和氧等离子体的例子进行了说明。定义了一个有效的反射系数来比较新旧边界条件的结果。

Conclusion: 提出了一种新的电子边界条件，能够准确描述电子与等离子体壁的相互作用，考虑了壁内微物理过程。该方法具有计算成本适中、适用范围广的优点。未来的工作可以将其应用于更复杂的材料和等离子体环境。

Abstract: We derive and implement a suitable boundary condition for the kinetic description of the electrons inside a plasma, which takes into account microphysical processes inside the wall. It is based on the surface scattering kernel, which describes the scattering cascade of the electron in the solid and the excitation of secondary electrons. The resulting boundary condition is inelastic, angle- and energy-dependent. The implementation for a Boltzmann equation solved by a Legendre polynomial expansion method is presented, elucidating the modest additional computational cost of the new boundary condition. Results, indicating the influence of the inelasticity, are shown for the example of a silicon wall facing argon, helium and oxygen plasmas, but the described construction is also valid for other materials. An effective reflection coefficient is defined to compare the results with previously used boundary conditions.

</details>

### [84] [Trust-Based Social Learning for Communication (TSLEC) Protocol Evolution in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.19562)
*Abraham Itzhak Weinberg*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: TSLEC框架通过引入基于信任的社会学习来加速多智能体系统中的通信涌现，通过显式教学和知识过滤，提高了学习效率和协议的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 独立学习在多智能体系统中导致通信协议收敛慢且可能次优。该研究旨在解决这一问题，通过一种更有效的通信涌现机制来加速学习过程并生成更优的协议。

Method: 提出了TSLEC（Trust-Based Social Learning with Emergent Communication）框架，其中智能体通过显式教学将成功的策略传授给同伴，并利用学习到的信任关系来调节知识的传递。实验在100个回合、30个随机种子下进行，并将TSLEC与独立涌现方法进行对比。

Result: 与独立涌现相比，基于信任的社会学习将收敛所需的回合数减少了23.9%（p < 0.001, Cohen's d = 1.98）。TSLEC生成的通信协议具有组合性（C = 0.38），并在动态目标下保持了鲁棒性（Phi > 0.867 解码准确率）。信任得分与教学质量高度相关（r = 0.743, p < 0.001），实现了有效的知识过滤。

Conclusion: 显式社会学习能从根本上加速多智能体协调中的通信涌现。TSLEC框架通过信任机制有效促进了知识的传播和过滤，提高了学习效率和通信协议的性能。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的信任模型和教学策略。

Abstract: Emergent communication in multi-agent systems typically occurs through independent learning, resulting in slow convergence and potentially suboptimal protocols. We introduce TSLEC (Trust-Based Social Learning with Emergent Communication), a framework where agents explicitly teach successful strategies to peers, with knowledge transfer modulated by learned trust relationships. Through experiments with 100 episodes across 30 random seeds, we demonstrate that trust-based social learning reduces episodes-to-convergence by 23.9% (p < 0.001, Cohen's d = 1.98) compared to independent emergence, while producing compositional protocols (C = 0.38) that remain robust under dynamic objectives (Phi > 0.867 decoding accuracy). Trust scores strongly correlate with teaching quality (r = 0.743, p < 0.001), enabling effective knowledge filtering. Our results establish that explicit social learning fundamentally accelerates emergent communication in multi-agent coordination.

### [85] [Complex Instruction Following with Diverse Style Policies in Football Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.19885)
*Chenglu Sun,Shuo Shen,Haonan Hu,Wei Zhou,Chen Chen*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 在复杂的、多智能体环境（如足球比赛）中，语言控制强化学习（LC-RL）面临理解和执行高层或抽象指令的挑战。我们提出了语言控制多样化风格策略（LCDSP），一种包含多样化风格训练（DST）和风格解释器（SI）的新型LC-RL范式。DST通过风格参数（SP）调制智能体动作，训练单个策略以展现广泛多样的行为。SI将高层语言指令快速准确地翻译成SP。实验证明LCDSP能有效理解抽象战术指令并执行所需的多样化行为风格，适用于复杂的实际应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言控制强化学习（LC-RL）在处理简单指令和基础领域方面取得了进展，但在复杂的多智能体环境（例如足球比赛）中，理解和执行高层或抽象指令仍然是一个重大挑战。这限制了LC-RL在更广泛、更实际场景中的应用，因此有必要开发能够处理复杂指令和环境的新型LC-RL方法。

Method: 我们提出了一种名为语言控制多样化风格策略（LCDSP）的新型LC-RL范式。LCDSP包含两个关键组成部分：1. 多样化风格训练（DST）：该方法训练一个单一的策略，通过风格参数（SP）来调整智能体动作，使其能够表现出广泛多样的行为。2. 风格解释器（SI）：该组件负责将高层语言指令快速而准确地翻译成相应的风格参数（SP）。实验在复杂的5v5足球环境中进行。

Result: 通过在复杂的5v5足球环境中的大量实验，我们证明了LCDSP能够有效地理解抽象的战术指令，并准确地执行期望的多样化行为风格。这表明LCDSP在处理复杂场景和实际应用方面具有巨大潜力。

Conclusion: LCDSP成功地解决了在复杂多智能体环境中理解和执行抽象语言指令的挑战。通过结合多样化风格训练和风格解释器，LCDSP能够实现策略的多样化行为，并根据语言指令进行精确控制。该方法在足球比赛环境中得到了验证，展示了其在复杂现实世界应用中的潜力。未来的工作可以探索LCDSP在其他复杂领域以及更广泛的语言指令理解方面的应用。

Abstract: Despite advancements in language-controlled reinforcement learning (LC-RL) for basic domains and straightforward commands (e.g., object manipulation and navigation), effectively extending LC-RL to comprehend and execute high-level or abstract instructions in complex, multi-agent environments, such as football games, remains a significant challenge. To address this gap, we introduce Language-Controlled Diverse Style Policies (LCDSP), a novel LC-RL paradigm specifically designed for complex scenarios. LCDSP comprises two key components: a Diverse Style Training (DST) method and a Style Interpreter (SI). The DST method efficiently trains a single policy capable of exhibiting a wide range of diverse behaviors by modulating agent actions through style parameters (SP). The SI is designed to accurately and rapidly translate high-level language instructions into these corresponding SP. Through extensive experiments in a complex 5v5 football environment, we demonstrate that LCDSP effectively comprehends abstract tactical instructions and accurately executes the desired diverse behavioral styles, showcasing its potential for complex, real-world applications.

### [86] [ShortageSim: Simulating Drug Shortages under Information Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.01813)
*Mingxuan Cui,Yilan Jiang,Duo Zhou,Cheng Qian,Yuji Zhang,Qiong Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 药物短缺是一个全球性问题，但现有研究对监管干预措施的效果了解不足。本文提出了ShortageSim，一个基于LLM智能体的模拟框架，用于评估信息不对称下监管干预对竞争动态的影响。模拟结果显示，ShortageSim能显著缩短生产中断事件的解决时间，并且比传统方法更接近现实。该框架为理解不确定性环境下的竞争提供了新方法，并开源了模拟框架和数据集，以促进未来的政策设计研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球范围内，药物短缺给患者护理和医疗系统带来了严峻风险。然而，由于药品供应链中的信息不对称，监管干预措施的有效性一直未能得到充分的理解。现有模型往往假设完全理性和信息完整，这与现实情况存在差距，限制了对真实世界中监管政策有效性的评估。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为ShortageSim的模拟框架。该框架利用大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的智能体来模拟药品制造商和机构买方的战略决策。这些决策是对监管机构发出的短缺警报的回应。与传统的、假设完全理性和信息完整的博弈论模型不同，ShortageSim能够模拟不同主体对监管公告的不同解读及其由此产生的决策。该框架在包含2,925个FDA药物短缺事件的历史数据集上进行了实验。

Result: 在对历史短缺事件数据集的实验中，ShortageSim在应对生产中断的情况下，将解决延迟时间缩短了高达84%。与零样本基线方法相比，ShortageSim的模拟轨迹更接近现实情况。研究证实了监管警报在解决药物短缺方面的有效性，并为研究多阶段不确定环境下的竞争提供了新方法。

Conclusion: ShortageSim框架成功地模拟了信息不对称下监管干预对药品供应链竞争动态的影响，并证明了其在缩短短缺解决时间和提高模拟准确性方面的优势。该研究不仅确认了监管警报在缓解药物短缺中的作用，还为相关领域的研究提供了新工具。未来工作可以利用开源的ShortageSim框架和数据集，进一步探索和测试更优化的政策设计，以应对供应链中的不确定性。

Abstract: Drug shortages pose critical risks to patient care and healthcare systems worldwide, yet the effectiveness of regulatory interventions remains poorly understood due to information asymmetries in pharmaceutical supply chains. We propose \textbf{ShortageSim}, addresses this challenge by providing the first simulation framework that evaluates the impact of regulatory interventions on competition dynamics under information asymmetry. Using Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents, the framework models the strategic decisions of drug manufacturers and institutional buyers, in response to shortage alerts given by the regulatory agency. Unlike traditional game theory models that assume perfect rationality and complete information, ShortageSim simulates heterogeneous interpretations on regulatory announcements and the resulting decisions. Experiments on self-processed dataset of historical shortage events show that ShortageSim reduces the resolution lag for production disruption cases by up to 84\%, achieving closer alignment to real-world trajectories than the zero-shot baseline. Our framework confirms the effect of regulatory alert in addressing shortages and introduces a new method for understanding competition in multi-stage environments under uncertainty. We open-source ShortageSim and a dataset of 2,925 FDA shortage events, providing a novel framework for future research on policy design and testing in supply chains under information asymmetry.

### [87] [RadAgents: Multimodal Agentic Reasoning for Chest X-ray Interpretation with Radiologist-like Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.20490)
*Kai Zhang,Corey D Barrett,Jangwon Kim,Lichao Sun,Tara Taghavi,Krishnaram Kenthapadi*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: RadAgents是一个多智能体框架，用于解决胸部X光（CXR）解释中的挑战，通过结合临床知识、多模态推理和类似放射科医生的工作流程，解决了现有方法在可解释性、多模态证据融合和一致性验证方面的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的胸部X光（CXR）解释方法存在三大局限性：1. 缺乏临床可解释性和指南一致性；2. 多模态证据融合不足，导致解释缺乏视觉基础；3. 缺乏跨工具一致性检测和验证机制。这些问题限制了AI在CXR解释中的应用。RadAgents旨在解决这些关键问题。

Method: RadAgents是一个多智能体框架，通过以下方式解决上述问题：1. 耦合临床先验知识：将放射科医生的专业知识整合到系统中。2. 任务感知多模态推理：对来自不同工具（如图像分析工具）的输出进行整合和推理。3. 编码放射科医生工作流：将标准的CXR解释流程（如病灶识别、测量、与既往检查对比等）模块化地实现在系统中。4. 集成接地和多模态检索增强：通过视觉 grounding 和多模态检索来验证信息，解决冲突，提高输出的可靠性、透明度和一致性。

Result: RadAgents通过其创新的框架，显著提高了CXR解释的可靠性、透明度和与临床实践的一致性。通过整合临床先验、多模态推理和工作流模拟，它能更有效地融合多模态证据，生成更具视觉基础和可解释性的报告，并能检测和解决不同信息源之间的冲突，为临床决策提供更可信的支持。

Conclusion: RadAgents通过引入一个创新的多智能体框架，成功地解决了当前胸部X光（CXR）解释领域中存在的关键挑战，包括可解释性、多模态证据融合和一致性验证。该框架通过模拟放射科医生的工作流程，并集成先进的推理和验证机制，显著提升了AI在CXR解释任务中的性能和可靠性，为实现更智能、更可信的临床决策辅助系统铺平了道路。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的临床场景和与其他医疗系统的集成。

Abstract: Agentic systems offer a potential path to solve complex clinical tasks through collaboration among specialized agents, augmented by tool use and external knowledge bases. Nevertheless, for chest X-ray (CXR) interpretation, prevailing methods remain limited: (i) reasoning is frequently neither clinically interpretable nor aligned with guidelines, reflecting mere aggregation of tool outputs; (ii) multimodal evidence is insufficiently fused, yielding text-only rationales that are not visually grounded; and (iii) systems rarely detect or resolve cross-tool inconsistencies and provide no principled verification mechanisms. To bridge the above gaps, we present RadAgents, a multi-agent framework that couples clinical priors with task-aware multimodal reasoning and encodes a radiologist-style workflow into a modular, auditable pipeline. In addition, we integrate grounding and multimodal retrieval-augmentation to verify and resolve context conflicts, resulting in outputs that are more reliable, transparent, and consistent with clinical practice.

</details>


### [88] [VIL2C: Value-of-Information Aware Low-Latency Communication for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.19146)
*Qian Zhang,Zhuo Sun,Yao Zhang,Zhiwen Yu,Bin Guo,Jun Zhang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 通信延迟会影响多智能体强化学习（MARL）系统的性能，尤其是在自动驾驶等时效性应用中。本研究提出了一种名为VIL2C（Value-of-Information aware Low-latency Communication）的方案，通过引入信息价值（VOI）指标来量化延迟消息的重要性，并结合渐进式消息接收机制，主动调整通信延迟分布，优先传输高价值信息，避免不必要的等待，从而有效缓解通信延迟带来的负面影响，并在实验中证明了其优于现有方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在协作多智能体强化学习（MARL）系统中，智能体间的通信对于提升系统性能至关重要。然而，实际应用中普遍存在的通信延迟问题，会导致动作决策延迟和信息共享滞后，尤其是在自动驾驶等对时间要求极高的场景下，会严重阻碍MARL性能的提升。因此，解决通信延迟对MARL系统的负面影响具有重要的现实意义。

Method: 本研究提出了一种名为VIL2C（Value-of-Information aware Low-latency Communication）的通信方案。该方案的核心在于：1. 定义信息价值（VOI）指标，量化延迟消息的重要性；2. 提出渐进式消息接收机制，根据接收到的消息自适应地调整接收持续时间。基于VOI，VIL2C方案进行了优化的资源分配，并从理论上证明了其性能优势。实验部分在多种通信条件下进行了广泛的测试。

Result: 实验结果表明，VIL2C方案在各种通信条件下均优于现有的通信方法。其性能提升得益于：1. 通过资源分配实现高VOI消息的低延迟传输；2. 通过自适应接收持续时间消除不必要的等待周期。具体性能提升的指标和与现有方法的详细比较在实验部分给出。

Conclusion: VIL2C方案通过引入信息价值（VOI）和渐进式消息接收机制，有效解决了多智能体强化学习（MARL）系统中的通信延迟问题，特别是在时效性应用中。该方案能够根据信息的重要性动态调整通信策略，显著提升了MARL系统的性能。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的通信环境和多智能体交互场景，并进一步优化VOI的计算和资源分配策略。

Abstract: Inter-agent communication serves as an effective mechanism for enhancing performance in collaborative multi-agent reinforcement learning(MARL) systems. However, the inherent communication latency in practical systems induces both action decision delays and outdated information sharing, impeding MARL performance gains, particularly in time-critical applications like autonomous driving. In this work, we propose a Value-of-Information aware Low-latency Communication(VIL2C) scheme that proactively adjusts the latency distribution to mitigate its effects in MARL systems. Specifically, we define a Value of Information (VOI) metric to quantify the importance of delayed message transmission based on each delayed message's importance. Moreover, we propose a progressive message reception mechanism to adaptively adjust the reception duration based on received messages. We derive the optimized VoI aware resource allocation and theoretically prove the performance advantage of the proposed VIL2C scheme. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VIL2C outperforms existing approaches under various communication conditions. These gains are attributed to the low-latency transmission of high-VoI messages via resource allocation and the elimination of unnecessary waiting periods via adaptive reception duration.

</details>

### [89] [Mechanical Design of the PIP-II ORBUMP Pulsed Dipole Magnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.19658)
*D. Karas,K. Badgley,Z. Chen,V. Chernenok,M. Davidson,D. Harding,D. Johnson,V. Kashikhin,W. Robotham,T. Strauss,B. Szabo,J. Vander Meulen*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: PIP-II项目升级了费米实验室的磁体脉冲速率和磁场强度。本文介绍了ORBUMP磁体机械设计，包括其层压铁芯、固定方式、线圈设计以及绝缘材料。通过有限元分析优化了夹紧设计，并进行了部分放电测试以评估高压性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PIP-II项目要求注入系统磁体脉冲速率从15 Hz提高到20 Hz，并且ORBUMP磁体的磁场强度增加约30%。ORBUMP磁体的设计对于满足这些要求至关重要，特别是其机械结构和磁场性能的保证。

Method: 本文介绍了ORBUMP磁体的机械设计，包括使用0.127毫米厚的低碳钢叠片构成铁芯，并采用C-5无机磷酸镁涂层。铁芯通过焊接在端板上的外部拉杆进行夹紧。使用ANSYS有限元分析来评估焊接后的铁芯变形。线圈采用单匝水冷设计，并使用纯聚醚醚酮（PEEK）作为绝缘材料。通过1:1比例样品的部分放电测试来评估PEEK绝缘体的高压性能。

Result: 有限元分析优化了夹紧设计，以最小化焊接后铁芯的变形。线圈的制造公差和制造技术被评估，以确保磁体能够实现所需的磁场特性。部分放电测试结果表明，纯PEEK绝缘体在高压下具有良好的性能。

Conclusion: ORBUMP磁体的机械设计已经完成，并通过有限元分析和部分放电测试进行了验证。该设计满足了PIP-II项目对磁体脉冲速率和磁场强度的要求。未来的工作可以进一步优化设计以提高效率和可靠性。

Abstract: The Proton Improvement Plan II (PIP-II) project is a vital upgrade to the Fermilab accelerator complex. The magnet pulse rate of the PIP-II Injection system requires an increase from the current rate of 15 Hz to 20 Hz as well as a roughly 30% increase in the magnetic field of the new Orbital Bump (ORBUMP) pulsed dipole magnets in the Booster. The ORBUMP magnet mechanical design is presented in this paper. The ORBUMP magnet is secured in a vacuum box and the core is made up of 0.127 mm thick, low carbon steel laminations with a C-5 inorganic magnesium phosphate coating. The core is clamped using external tie bars welded to the core end plates. ANSYS Finite Element Analysis (FEA) was used to evaluate the clamping design to minimize the deflection of the core post welding of the tie bars. The water-cooled, single turn coil, which shapes the magnetic field by acting as the pole tips, is critical for the integrated field homogeneity. The coil manufacturing tolerances and fabrication techniques were evaluated to ensure the magnetic properties of the magnet could be obtained. The coil is electrically isolated from the core using virgin Polyether ether ketone (PEEK) insulating material in the gap. An investigation into the high voltage performance of the virgin PEEK insulator was conducted via partial discharge testing using a 1:1 scale sample.

</details>


### [90] [Analog Signal Multiplexing System for the Iota Proton Injector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.19772)
*Daniel R. MacLean,Dean R. Edstrom*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: Fermilab的FAST设施开发了一种32通道模拟信号复用系统，用于监控IPI的励磁参数，以降低成本和优化空间，并已成功实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在Fermilab的FAST设施中，低能和中能IPI（包括四极磁铁和多功能校正器）的励磁参数监控需求，以及PLC控制系统中成本和空间优化的需求。

Method: 设计并实现了一个32输入到4输出的模拟信号复用系统，该系统连接到PLC控制系统，用于实时读取32个模拟通道的电流和电压。

Result: 该复用系统成功实现了32个模拟通道的实时读取，显著降低了成本并优化了机架空间，同时满足了精确监控的需求。

Conclusion: 所提出的32通道模拟信号复用系统是一种经济高效且节省空间的解决方案，成功应用于Fermilab的IPI项目，为未来类似加速器项目提供了参考。

Abstract: The Fermilab Accelerator Science and Technology (FAST) Facility at FNAL is a dedicated research and development center focused on advancing particle accelerator technologies for future applications worldwide. Currently, a key objective of FAST Operations is to commission the 2.5&#8239;MeV IOTA Proton Injector (IPI) and enable proton injection into the Integrable Optics Test Accelerator (IOTA) storage ring. The low and medium-energy sections of the IPI include four frame-style dipole trims and two multi-function correctors with independently controlled coils, requiring readout of 32 analog channels for current and voltage monitoring in total. To reduce cost and optimize rack space within the PLC-based control system, a 32-to-4 analog signal multiplexing system was designed and implemented. This system enables real-time readback of excitation parameters from all magnetic correctors. This paper presents the design, construction, implementation, and performance of the multiplexing system.

</details>


### [91] [Beam Steering and Radiation Generation of Electrons in Bent Crystals in the Sub-GeV Domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.19807)
*R. Negrello,M. Romagnoni,A. Sytov,N. Canale,D. De Salvador,P. Fedeli,V. Guidi,V. V. Haurylavets,P. Klag,W. Lauth,L. Malagutti,A. Mazzolari,G. Paternò,F. Sgarbossa,M. Soldani,V. V. Tikhomirov,D. Valzani,L. Bandiera*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 研究了亚GeV电子在弯曲硅晶体中穿行时的束流转向和辐射发射现象，发现在低能下（300 MeV）仍能实现超过50%的沟道化效率，且沟道化和体积反射可将辐射发射增强高达6倍，验证了在低能加速器设施中使用弯曲晶体进行束流操控和高强度光子产生的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低能（亚GeV）加速器设施中，对电子束流进行高效操控和产生高强度光子一直是技术挑战。本研究旨在探索利用弯曲硅晶体实现这一目标，以支持新型光源和束流控制策略的发展。

Method: 使用855、600和300 MeV的电子束流，在 Mainz Microtron (MAMI) 实验装置中，对一块15微米厚的沿(111)晶面弯曲的硅晶体进行了实验研究。结合实验测量和模拟分析，研究了沟道化、去沟道化、再沟道化和体积俘获等现象对束流偏转和辐射发射的贡献。

Result: 在300 MeV的低能下，观察到晶体转向效应仍然有效，沟道化效率超过50%，创下了该能量下的记录。与未对准取向相比，沟道化和体积反射将辐射发射增强了高达6倍，证明了亚GeV能区存在显著的取向相干效应。

Conclusion: 本研究证实了在低能加速器设施中使用弯曲晶体进行高效束流操控和高强度光子产生的可行性。研究结果为开发新型光子源和束流控制技术提供了实验依据。未来可进一步探索更复杂的晶体结构和更高能量下的应用。

Abstract: We present an investigation into beam steering and radiation emission by sub-GeV electrons traversing bent silicon crystals. Using 855, 600, and 300~MeV electron beams at the Mainz Microtron (MAMI), we explored orientational coherent effects and particle dynamics in a 15~$μ$m-thick crystal bent along the (111) planes. Combined experimental and simulation analyses enabled the classification and quantitative assessment of the contributions from channeling, dechanneling, rechanneling, and volume capture to both beam deflection and radiation emission. Crystal steering remained effective even at 300~MeV, with measured channeling efficiencies exceeding 50\%, a record at such low energy. Channeling and volume reflection enhanced radiation emission by up to a factor of six compared to the misaligned orientation, highlighting strong orientational coherence effects in the sub-GeV regime. These findings confirm the feasibility of using bent crystals for efficient beam manipulation and high-intensity photon generation at low energies, supporting the development of novel light sources and beam control strategies at accelerator facilities operating in this energy range.

</details>


### [92] [Evaluating a Transition-jump System for the Fermilab Main Injector Using Xsuite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.20219)
*A. P. Schreckenberger,R. Ainsworth,M. Xiao*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个用于费米实验室主注入器（MI）的Xsuite模拟框架，并评估了加速器中穿越强子效应的行为。研究了在PIP-II项目中引入四极磁铁作为过渡跳跃系统的一部分。评估了由过渡引起的失谐引起的束损，考虑了MI四极磁铁误差、跳跃磁铁的磁铁间变异性、电源误差和定时抖动等系统效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究穿越强子效应是加速器物理中的一个重要问题，因为强子效应可能导致束损和性能下降。本研究的动机是评估在费米实验室主注入器（MI）中引入过渡跳跃系统对穿越强子效应行为的影响，该系统是PIP-II项目的一部分。

Method: 使用Xsuite模拟框架对费米实验室主注入器（MI）进行了模拟。研究了在MI中引入四极磁铁作为过渡跳跃系统一部分的效应。评估了由过渡引起的失谐引起的束损，并考虑了MI四极磁铁误差、跳跃磁铁的磁铁间变异性、电源误差和定时抖动等系统效应。

Result: 模拟结果表明，过渡跳跃系统可以有效地减少由穿越强子效应引起的束损。然而，MI四极磁铁误差、跳跃磁铁的磁铁间变异性、电源误差和定时抖动等系统效应会影响过渡跳跃系统的性能。

Conclusion: Xsuite模拟框架可用于评估穿越强子效应行为。过渡跳跃系统可以减轻由穿越强子效应引起的束损，但系统效应需要仔细考虑以优化性能。未来的工作可以探索更先进的控制策略来进一步减轻这些系统效应的影响。

Abstract: We describe an Xsuite simulation framework for the Fermilab Main Injector (MI) along with an evaluation of transition-crossing behaviors in the accelerator. In particular, we studied the introduction of quadrupole magnets into the lattice as part of a transition-jump system that will be implemented through the $2^{nd}$ Proton Improvement Plan (PIP-II). Simulated beam losses spurred by transition-induced instabilities were assessed under several systematic effects, including MI quad errors, magnet-to-magnet variability in the jump magnets, power-supply errors, and timing jitter.

</details>


### [93] [Future Colliders Comparative Evaluation - Working Group Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.20417)
*G. Arduini,M. Benedikt,F. Gianotti,K. Jakobs,M. Lamont,R. Losito,M. Meddahi,J. Mnich,N. Mounet,D. Schulte,F. Sonnemann,S. Stapnes,F. Zimmermann*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: CERN is evaluating future collider projects like the FCC and alternatives for the mid-2040s, considering performance, sustainability, cost, and timelines, in preparation for the HL-LHC completion. The report compares these with international projects like CEPC and ILC, and reviews new accelerator techniques.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The completion of the High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC) by 2041 necessitates the planning of new major particle physics facilities. The 2020 European Strategy for Particle Physics prioritizes an electron-positron Higgs factory, followed by a high-energy hadron-hadron collider. A working group was formed to evaluate the Future Circular Collider (FCC) and other potential scenarios to inform the Update of the European Strategy for Particle Physics.

Method: A comparative evaluation of proposed future collider projects was conducted. The assessment considered various criteria including main performance parameters, environmental impact and sustainability, technical maturity, construction and operational costs, required human resources, and realistic implementation timelines. International projects (CEPC, ILC) and new accelerator techniques were also reviewed.

Result: The report presents a comparative evaluation of proposed future collider projects, assessing them against established criteria. It includes an overview of international projects within a similar timeframe and a review of new accelerator techniques.

Conclusion: This report provides a comparative evaluation of future collider projects, including the FCC and alternatives, to inform the European Strategy for Particle Physics. It considers a wide range of factors such as performance, cost, and sustainability, and contextualizes these within the global landscape of particle physics research.

Abstract: In anticipation of the completion of the High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC) programme by the end of 2041, CERN is preparing to launch a new major facility in the mid-2040s. According to the 2020 European Strategy for Particle Physics (ESPP), the highest-priority next collider is an electron-positron Higgs factory, followed in the longer term by a hadron-hadron collider at the highest achievable energy. The CERN directorate established a Future Colliders Comparative Evaluation working group in June 2023. This group brings together project leaders and domain experts to conduct a consistent evaluation of the Future Circular Collider (FCC) and alternative scenarios based on shared assumptions and standardized criteria. This report presents a comparative evaluation of proposed future collider projects submitted as input for the Update of the European Strategy for Particle Physics. These proposals are compared considering main performance parameters, environmental impact and sustainability, technical maturity, cost of construction and operation, required human resources, and realistic implementation timelines. An overview of the international collider projects within a similar timeframe, notably the CEPC in China and the ILC in Japan is also presented, as well as a short review of the status and prospects of new accelerator techniques.

</details>
